   var readOnlyRequest;
		var cn = "read-only";
		var cacheBusterParam = "?cb=" + Math.floor(Date.now() / 60000); // update every minute
		var setReadOnly = function () {
			document.body.className = (document.body.className === '') ? cn : document.body.className + ' ' + cn;
		};
		if (window.XMLHttpRequest) {
			readOnlyRequest = new XMLHttpRequest();
		} else if (window.ActiveXObject) {
			readOnlyRequest = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
		}
		readOnlyRequest.onreadystatechange = function() {
			if (readOnlyRequest.readyState == 4 &amp;&amp; readOnlyRequest.status &gt;= 500 &amp;&amp; readOnlyRequest.status &lt; 600) {
				setReadOnly();
			}
		};
    	readOnlyRequest.open('GET', "/ajax/readOnlyMode" + cacheBusterParam);
    	readOnlyRequest.send();
  </script>

            <p data-textannotation-id="93b5e16d7e51ecda39555018d96fbe36">
             Anyone with even a passing interest in cooking knows that
             <a data-amazonasin="B00FUF5OIS" data-amazonsubtag="[p|1673220904[a|B00FUF5OIS[au|5856732741879800112" data-amazontag="lifehackeramzn-20" href="http://www.amazon.com/dp/B00FUF5OIS/?m=ATVPDKIKX0DERascsubtag=[referrer|deals.kinja.com[t|link[p|1672680960[a|B00FUF5OIS[au|5727177402741770316&amp;tag=lifehackeramzn-20&amp;ascsubtag=[t|link[p|1673220904[a|B00FUF5OIS[au|5856732741879800112" onclick="window.ga('send', 'event', 'Commerce', 'lifehacker - Sub-$20 Sony Headphones, All-Clad Discounts, Cheap Luggage, More Deals', 'B00FUF5OIS');" target="_blank">
              All-Clad
             </a>
             is the most highly-regarded brand in kitchenware. In fact, if you poke your head behind the scenes of your favorite restaurants, chances are very good you'll see see their logo. If you're ready to level up your own cooking, several of their most popular items are on sale right now.
            </p>
            <p data-textannotation-id="0ff9b83b9592ecb38dab3c397797c8f4">
             I own that
             <a data-amazonasin="B00FUF5OIS" data-amazonsubtag="[p|1673220904[a|B00FUF5OIS[au|5856732741879800112" data-amazontag="lifehackeramzn-20" href="http://www.amazon.com/dp/B00FUF5OIS/?m=ATVPDKIKX0DERascsubtag=[referrer|deals.kinja.com[t|link[p|1672680960[a|B00FUF5OIS[au|5727177402741770316&amp;tag=lifehackeramzn-20&amp;ascsubtag=[t|link[p|1673220904[a|B00FUF5OIS[au|5856732741879800112" onclick="window.ga('send', 'event', 'Commerce', 'lifehacker - Sub-$20 Sony Headphones, All-Clad Discounts, Cheap Luggage, More Deals', 'B00FUF5OIS');" target="_blank">
              10" fry pan
             </a>
             , and it's as good as advertised, but the
             <a data-amazonasin="B00FUF5K8W" data-amazonsubtag="[p|1673220904[a|B00FUF5K8W[au|5856732741879800112" data-amazontag="lifehackeramzn-20" href="http://www.amazon.com/dp/B00FUF5K8W/?m=ATVPDKIKX0DERascsubtag=[referrer|deals.kinja.com[t|link[p|1672680960[a|B00FUF5K8W[au|5727177402741770316&amp;tag=lifehackeramzn-20&amp;ascsubtag=[t|link[p|1673220904[a|B00FUF5K8W[au|5856732741879800112" onclick="window.ga('send', 'event', 'Commerce', 'lifehacker - Sub-$20 Sony Headphones, All-Clad Discounts, Cheap Luggage, More Deals', 'B00FUF5K8W');" target="_blank">
              12" might make more sense
             </a>
             if you frequently cook larger meals. I haven't tried the
             <a data-amazonasin="B005GFYH6M" data-amazonsubtag="[p|1673220904[a|B005GFYH6M[au|5856732741879800112" data-amazontag="lifehackeramzn-20" href="http://www.amazon.com/dp/B005GFYH6M/?m=ATVPDKIKX0DERascsubtag=[referrer|deals.kinja.com[t|link[p|1672680960[a|B005GFYH6M[au|5727177402741770316&amp;tag=lifehackeramzn-20&amp;ascsubtag=[t|link[p|1673220904[a|B005GFYH6M[au|5856732741879800112" onclick="window.ga('send', 'event', 'Commerce', 'lifehacker - Sub-$20 Sony Headphones, All-Clad Discounts, Cheap Luggage, More Deals', 'B005GFYH6M');" target="_blank">
              saucepans
             </a>
             ,
             <a data-amazonasin="B004T6J9QC" data-amazonsubtag="[p|1673220904[a|B004T6J9QC[au|5856732741879800112" data-amazontag="lifehackeramzn-20" href="http://www.amazon.com/All-Clad-Stainless-Dishwasher-Stockpot-Cookware/dp/B004T6J9QC/ref=sr_1_2?s=home-garden&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1418913672&amp;sr=1-2&amp;keywords=all+clad+stock+potascsubtag=[referrer|deals.kinja.com[t|link[p|1672680960[a|B004T6J9QC[au|5727177402741770316&amp;tag=lifehackeramzn-20&amp;ascsubtag=[t|link[p|1673220904[a|B004T6J9QC[au|5856732741879800112" onclick="window.ga('send', 'event', 'Commerce', 'lifehacker - Sub-$20 Sony Headphones, All-Clad Discounts, Cheap Luggage, More Deals', 'B004T6J9QC');" target="_blank">

             , but they have ridiculous 4.8 star review averages, so suffice it to say, they should be good.
            </p>
            <p data-textannotation-id="77f90e32b2f2fdd01970cef5562388f0">
             So what makes All-Clad so great? These pans all have a three-layer construction that wraps a fast-heating aluminum core around a layer of durable and heat-retaining stainless steel. Plus, all of their products are made in America, and come with a lifetime warranty. Yes, they're expensive up-front, but if you take good care of them, you'll never need to buy pans again.
            </p>
